<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
 <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <title>O365 CORS Sample</title>
    <style> 
      body { 
        font-family:'Segoe UI'; 
      } 

      .paddedElement {
        margin-top: 5px; 
      }

      .hidden {
        visibility: hidden; 
      }
    </style>
   
</head>
<body>

   <h2>File</h2>
    <label for="TxtOauthToken">OAuth Token: </label><input type="text" id="TxtOauthToken" size="80"/>
    <br />
    <label for="endpointUrl">Endpoint URL: </label><input type="text" id="endpoint" size="80" /> 
    <br />
    <input type="button" class="paddedElement" id="getToken" value="Get Token"> 
    <input type="button" class="paddedElement" id="doCors" value="Make CORS Request" visibility="hidden" />
    <br /> 
    <br />
    <label for="results" class="hidden paddedElement" id="resultHeading">Results: </label>
    <br />
    <label id="debugMessage"></label>
    <pre id="results"></pre>
    <script type="text/javascript"> 
    // https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/office/office365/howto/create-web-apps-using-cors-to-access-files-in-office-365
      (function (window) { 
        var isCorsCompatible = function() {
          try
          {
              var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
              xhr.open("GET", getEndpointUrl());
              xhr.setRequestHeader("authorization", "Bearer " + token);
              xhr.setRequestHeader("accept", "application/json");
              xhr.onload = function () {
                 // CORS is working.
                 console.log("Browser is CORS compatible."); 
              }
              xhr.send();
          }
          catch (e)
          {
              if (e.number == -2147024891)
              {
                  console.log("Internet Explorer users must use Internet Explorer 11 with MS15-032: Cumulative security update for Internet Explorer (KB3038314) installed for this sample to work.");
              }
              else
              {
                  console.log("An unexpected error occurred. Please refresh the page."); 
              }

          }
        };

        var urlParameterExtraction = new (function () { 
          function splitQueryString(queryStringFormattedString) { 
            var split = queryStringFormattedString.split('&'); 

            // If there are no parameters in URL, do nothing.
            if (split == "") {
              return {};
            } 

            var results = {}; 

            // If there are parameters in URL, extract key/value pairs. 
            for (var i = 0; i < split.length; ++i) { 
              var p = split[i].split('=', 2); 
              if (p.length == 1) 
                results[p[0]] = ""; 
              else 
                results[p[0]] = decodeURIComponent(p[1].replace(/\+/g, " ")); 
            } 

            return results; 
          } 

          // Split the query string (after removing preceding '#'). 
          this.queryStringParameters = splitQueryString(window.location.hash.substr(1)); 
        })(); 

        var token = urlParameterExtraction.queryStringParameters['access_token']; 

        if (token == undefined) {
          document.getElementById("TxtOauthToken").value = "Click \"Get Token\" to trigger sign-in after entering the endpoint you want to use."; 

          document.getElementById("doCors").style.visibility = "hidden"; 
        }
        else {
          document.getElementById("TxtOauthToken").value = token;
          document.getElementById("doCors").style.visibility = "visible"; 
          document.getElementById("getToken").style.display = "none"; 
        }

        // Constructs the authentication URL and directs the user to it. 
        function requestToken() {
          
          // Change clientId and replyUrl to reflect your app's values 
          // found on the Configure tab in the Azure Management Portal.
          var clientId    = '45b92b9b-301e-4a83-9669-94477cdc8892';
          var replyUrl    = 'https://mycanvastristatedemo.herokuapp.com/';// https://tony-ren-dev.github.io/index2.html         https://tony-ren-dev.github.io/index2.html  https://tony-ren-dev.github.io/
          var resource    = "https://tonyren-my.sharepoint.com";

          var authServer  = 'https://login.windows.net/common/oauth2/authorize?'; 
          var endpointUrl = getEndpointUrl();
          //'https://tonyren-my.sharepoint.com/_api/v1.0/me/files'; 
          //https://tonyren-my.sharepoint.com/_api/v2.0/me/drive/root/children?expand=thumbnails

          var responseType = 'token'; 

          var url = authServer + 
                    "response_type=" + encodeURI(responseType) + "&" + 
                    "client_id=" + encodeURI(clientId) + "&" + 
                    "resource=" + encodeURI(resource) + "&" + 
                    "redirect_uri=" + encodeURI(replyUrl); 

          window.location = url; 
        } 

        document.getElementById("getToken").onclick = requestToken; 

        function getEndpointUrl() { 
          return document.getElementById("endpoint").value; 
        } 

        function getFilesFromO365() { 
          document.getElementById("results").textContent = ""; 

          // Check browser compatbility. Check console output for details.
          isCorsCompatible(); 

          try 
          { 
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest(); 
            xhr.open("GET", getEndpointUrl()); 

            // The APIs require an OAuth access token in the Authorization header, formatted like this: 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'. 
            xhr.setRequestHeader("Authorization", "Bearer " + token); 

            // Process the response from the API.  
            xhr.onload = function () { 
              document.getElementById("resultHeading").style.visibility = "visible"; 

              if (xhr.status == 200) { 
                var formattedResponse = JSON.stringify(JSON.parse(xhr.response), undefined, 2);
                document.getElementById("results").textContent = formattedResponse; 
              } else { 
                document.getElementById("results").textContent = "HTTP " + xhr.status + "<br>" + xhr.response; 
              } 
            } 

            // Make request.
            xhr.send(); 
          } 
          catch (err) 
          { 
            document.getElementById("resultHeading").style.visibility = "visible"; 
            document.getElementById("results").textContent = "Exception: " + err.message; 
          } 
        } 

        document.getElementById("doCors").onclick = getFilesFromO365; 

      })(window); 
    </script> 
  
  
</body>

                        <b:includable id='threaded_comment_js' var='post'>
                            <script async='async' expr:src='data:post.commentSrc' type='text/javascript' />

                            <script type='text/javascript'>
                                (function() {
                                    var items = < data: post.commentJso / > ;
                                    var msgs = < data: post.commentMsgs / > ;
                                    var config = < data: post.commentConfig / > ;

                                    // <![CDATA[
                                    var cursor = null;
                                    if (items && items.length > 0) {
                                        cursor = parseInt(items[items.length - 1].timestamp) + 1;
                                    }

                                    var bodyFromEntry = function(entry) {
                                        if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                                            for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                                                if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.contentRemoved') {
                                                    return '<span class="deleted-comment">' + entry.content.$t + '</span>';
                                                }
                                            }
                                        }
                                        return entry.content.$t;
                                    }

                                    var parse = function(data) {
                                        cursor = null;
                                        var comments = [];
                                        if (data && data.feed && data.feed.entry) {
                                            for (var i = 0, entry; entry = data.feed.entry[i]; i++) {
                                                var comment = {};
                                                // comment ID, parsed out of the original id format
                                                var id = /blog-(\d+).post-(\d+)/.exec(entry.id.$t);
                                                comment.id = id ? id[2] : null;
                                                comment.body = bodyFromEntry(entry);
                                                comment.timestamp = Date.parse(entry.published.$t) + '';
                                                if (entry.author && entry.author.constructor === Array) {
                                                    var auth = entry.author[0];
                                                    if (auth) {
                                                        comment.author = {
                                                            name: (auth.name ? auth.name.$t : undefined),
                                                            profileUrl: (auth.uri ? auth.uri.$t : undefined),
                                                            avatarUrl: (auth.gd$image ? auth.gd$image.src : undefined)
                                                        };
                                                    }
                                                }
                                                if (entry.link) {
                                                    if (entry.link[2]) {
                                                        comment.link = comment.permalink = entry.link[2].href;
                                                    }
                                                    if (entry.link[3]) {
                                                        var pid = /.*comments\/default\/(\d+)\?.*/.exec(entry.link[3].href);
                                                        if (pid && pid[1]) {
                                                            comment.parentId = pid[1];
                                                        }
                                                    }
                                                }
                                                comment.deleteclass = 'item-control blog-admin';
                                                if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                                                    for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                                                        if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.itemClass') {
                                                            comment.deleteclass += ' ' + entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                                                        } else if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.displayTime') {
                                                            comment.displayTime = entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                                                        }
                                                    }
                                                }
                                                comments.push(comment);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        return comments;
                                    };

                                    var paginator = function(callback) {
                                        if (hasMore()) {
                                            var url = config.feed + '?alt=json&v=2&orderby=published&reverse=false&max-results=50';
                                            if (cursor) {
                                                url += '&published-min=' + new Date(cursor).toISOString();
                                            }
                                            window.bloggercomments = function(data) {
                                                var parsed = parse(data);
                                                cursor = parsed.length < 50 ? null :
                                                    parseInt(parsed[parsed.length - 1].timestamp) + 1
                                                callback(parsed);
                                                window.bloggercomments = null;
                                            }
                                            url += '&callback=bloggercomments';
                                            var script = document.createElement('script');
                                            script.type = 'text/javascript';
                                            script.src = url;
                                            document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
                                        }
                                    };
                                    var hasMore = function() {
                                        return !!cursor;
                                    };
                                    var getMeta = function(key, comment) {
                                        if ('iswriter' == key) {
                                            var matches = !!comment.author &&
                                                comment.author.name == config.authorName &&
                                                comment.author.profileUrl == config.authorUrl;
                                            return matches ? 'true' : '';
                                        } else if ('deletelink' == key) {
                                            return config.baseUri + '/delete-comment.g?blogID=' +
                                                config.blogId + '&postID=' + comment.id;
                                        } else if ('deleteclass' == key) {
                                            return comment.deleteclass;
                                        }
                                        return '';
                                    };

                                    var replybox = null;
                                    var replyUrlParts = null;
                                    var replyParent = undefined;

                                    var onReply = function(commentId, domId) {
                                        if (replybox == null) {
                                            // lazily cache replybox, and adjust to suit this style:
                                            replybox = document.getElementById('comment-editor');
                                            if (replybox != null) {
                                                replybox.height = '250px';
                                                replybox.style.display = 'block';
                                                replyUrlParts = replybox.src.split('#');
                                            }
                                        }
                                        if (replybox && (commentId !== replyParent)) {
                                            document.getElementById(domId).insertBefore(document.getElementById('form-wrapper'), null);
                                            replybox.src = replyUrlParts[0] +
                                                (commentId ? '&parentID=' + commentId : '') +
                                                '#' + replyUrlParts[1];
                                            replyParent = commentId;
                                        }
                                    };

                                    var hash = (window.location.hash || '#').substring(1);
                                    var startThread, targetComment;
                                    if (/^comment-form_/.test(hash)) {
                                        startThread = hash.substring('comment-form_'.length);
                                    } else if (/^c[0-9]+$/.test(hash)) {
                                        targetComment = hash.substring(1);
                                    }

                                    // Configure commenting API:
                                    var configJso = {
                                        'maxDepth': config.maxThreadDepth
                                    };
                                    var provider = {
                                        'id': config.postId,
                                        'data': items,
                                        'loadNext': paginator,
                                        'hasMore': hasMore,
                                        'getMeta': getMeta,
                                        'onReply': onReply,
                                        'rendered': true,
                                        'initComment': targetComment,
                                        'initReplyThread': startThread,
                                        'config': configJso,
                                        'messages': msgs
                                    };

                                    var render = function() {
                                        if (window.goog && window.goog.comments) {
                                            var holder = document.getElementById('comment-holder');
                                            window.goog.comments.render(holder, provider);
                                        }
                                    };

                                    // render now, or queue to render when library loads:
                                    if (window.goog && window.goog.comments) {
                                        render();
                                    } else {
                                        window.goog = window.goog || {};
                                        window.goog.comments = window.goog.comments || {};
                                        window.goog.comments.loadQueue = window.goog.comments.loadQueue || [];
                                        window.goog.comments.loadQueue.push(render);
                                    }
                                })();
                                // ]]>
                            </script>
                        </b:includable>
                        <b:includable id='threaded_comments' var='post'>
                            <div class='comments' id='comments'>
                                <a name='comments' />
                                <h4>

        1 <data:commentLabel/>:
      <b:else/>
        <data:post.numComments/> <data:commentLabelPlural/>:
      </b:if>

                                </p>

                                <b:if cond='data:showCmtPopup'>
                                    <div id='comment-popup'>
                                        <iframe allowtransparency='true' frameborder='0' id='comment-actions' name='comment-actions' scrolling='no'>
        </iframe>
                                    </div>
                                </b:if>

                                <div id='backlinks-container'>
                                    <div expr:id='data:widget.instanceId + &quot;_backlinks-container&quot;'>
                                        <b:if cond='data:post.showBacklinks'>

                        //<![CDATA[
                        function resizeThumb(e, b) {
                            var c = document.getElementById(e),
                                d = c.getElementsByTagName("img");
                            for (var a = 0; a < d.length; a++) {
                                d[a].src = d[a].src.replace(/\/s72\-c/, "/s" + b + "-c");
                                d[a].width = b
                            }
                        }
                        resizeThumb("main", 180);
                        //]]>
                    </script>

                    <script type='text/javascript'>
                        //<![CDATA[
                        (function() {
                            var a = $(".blog-posts.hfeed").find(".post"),
                                c = $("#view .grid"),
                                d = $("#view .list");

                            function b() {
                                a.addClass("grid");
                                c.addClass("active");
                                d.removeClass("active");
                                createCookie("grid", null, 7000);
                                return false
                            }

                            function e() {
                                a.removeClass("grid");
                                c.removeClass("active");
                                d.addClass("active");
                                eraseCookie("grid");
                                return false
                            }
                            if (readCookie("grid")) {
                                b();
                                eraseCookie("grid")
                            } else {
                                e()
                            }
                            c.click(b);
                            d.click(e)
                        })();

                        function createCookie(c, d, e) {
                            if (e) {
                                var b = new Date();
                                b.setTime(b.getTime() + (e * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                                var a = "; expires=" + b.toGMTString()
                            } else {
                                var a = ""
                            }
                            document.cookie = c + "=" + d + a + "; path=/"
                        }

                        function readCookie(b) {
                            var e = b + "=";
                            var a = document.cookie.split(";");
                            for (var d = 0; d < a.length; d++) {
                                var f = a[d];
                                while (f.charAt(0) == " ") {
                                    f = f.substring(1, f.length)
                                }
                                if (f.indexOf(e) == 0) {
                                    return f.substring(e.length, f.length)
                                }
                            }
                            return null
                        }

                        function eraseCookie(a) {
                            createCookie(a, "", -1)
                        };
                        //]]>
                    </script>
                </b:if>

                //<![CDATA[
                var pageCount = 6;
                var displayPageNum = 3;
                var upPageWord = 'Â« Previous'
                var downPageWord = 'Next Â»';

                function showpageCount(x) {
                    var C = home_page_url;
                    var E = new Array();
                    var y = 1;
                    var H = 1;
                    var v = 0;
                    var p = 0;
                    var G = 0;
                    var F = "";
                    var J = "";
                    var w = "";
                    for (var z = 0, A; A = x.feed.entry[z]; z++) {
                        var u = A.published.$t.substring(0, 19) + A.published.$t.substring(23, 29);
                        timestamp = encodeURIComponent(u);
                        var i = A.title.$t;
                        if (i != "") {
                            if (v == 0 || (v % pageCount == (pageCount - 1))) {
                                if (C.indexOf(timestamp) != -1) {
                                    y = H
                                }
                                if (i != "") {
                                    H++
                                }
                                E[E.length] = "/search?updated-max=" + timestamp + "&max-results=" + pageCount
                            }
                        }
                        v++
                    }
                    for (var D = 0; D < E.length; D++) {
                        if (D >= (y - displayPageNum - 1) && D < (y + displayPageNum)) {
                            if (p == 0 && D == y - 2) {
                                if (y == 2) {
                                    J = '<span class="showpage"><a href="/">' + upPageWord + "</a></span>"
                                } else {
                                    J = '<span class="showpage"><a href="' + E[D] + '">' + upPageWord + "</a></span>"
                                }
                                p++
                            }
                            if (D == (y - 1)) {
                                F += '<span class="showpagePoint">' + y + "</span>"
                            } else {
                                if (D == 0) {
                                    F += '<span class="showpageNum"><a href="/">1</a></span>'
                                } else {
                                    F += '<span class="showpageNum"><a href="' + E[D] + '">' + (D + 1) + "</a></span>"
                                }
                            }
                            if (G == 0 && D == y) {
                                w = '<span class="showpage"> <a href="' + E[D] + '">' + downPageWord + "</a></span>";
                                G++
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    if (y > 1) {
                        F = "" + J + " " + F + " "
                    }
                    F = '<div class="showpageArea">' + F;
                    if (y < (H - 1)) {
                        F += w
                    }
                    if (H == 1) {
                        H++
                    }
                    F += "</div>";
                    var I = document.getElementsByName("pageArea");
                    var B = document.getElementById("blog-pager");
                    if (H <= 2) {
                        F = ""
                    }
                    for (var D = 0; D < I.length; D++) {
                        I[D].innerHTML = F
                    }
                    if (I && I.length > 0) {
                        F = ""
                    }
                    if (B) {
                        B.innerHTML = F
                    }
                }

                function showpageCount2(A) {
                    var F = home_page_url;
                    var G = new Array();
                    var J = F.indexOf("/search/label/") != -1;
                    var M = J ? F.substr(F.indexOf("/search/label/") + 14, F.length) : "";
                    M = M.indexOf("?") != -1 ? M.substr(0, M.indexOf("?")) : M;
                    var B = 1;
                    var L = 1;

                    var p = 0;
                    var K = 0;
                    var I = "";
                    var P = "";

                    var N = '<span class="showpageNum"><a href="/search/label/' + M + "?&max-results=" + pageCount + '">';
                    var F = home_page_url;

                        timestamp = encodeURIComponent(x);

                        if (i != "") {

                                if (F.indexOf(timestamp) != -1) {
                                    B = L

                                    L++
                                }

                        y++

                            if (p == 0 && H == B - 2) {
                                if (B == 2) {
                                    P = N + upPageWord + "</a></span>"
                                } else {
                                    P = '<span class="showpage"><a href="' + G[H] + '">' + upPageWord + "</a></span>"
                                }
                                p++
                            }
                            if (H == (B - 1)) {
                                I += '<span class="showpagePoint">' + B + "</span>"
                            } else {
                                if (H == 0) {
                                    I = N + "1</a></span>"
                                } else {
                                    I += '<span class="showpageNum"><a href="' + G[H] + '">' + (H + 1) + "</a></span>"
                                }
                            }

                                K++
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    if (B > 1) {
                        if (!J) {
                            I = "" + P + " " + I + " "
                        } else {
                            I = "" + P + " " + I + " "
                        }
                    }
                    I = '<div class="showpageArea">' + I;
                    if (B < (L - 1)) {
                        I += z
                    }
                    if (L == 1) {
                        L++
                    }
                    I += "</div>";
                    var O = document.getElementsByName("pageArea");
                    var E = document.getElementById("blog-pager");
                    if (L <= 2) {
                        I = ""

                var home_page_url = location.href;
                var thisUrl = home_page_url;

                    if (thisUrl.indexOf("?updated-max") != -1) {

                    } else {

                    }
                }
                var home_page = "/";
                if (thisUrl.indexOf("?q=") == -1) {

                        document.write('<script src="' + home_page + 'feeds/posts/summary?alt=json-in-script&callback=showpageCount&max-results=99999" ><\/script>')
                    } else {
                        document.write('<script src="' + home_page + "feeds/posts/full/-/" + lblname1 + '?alt=json-in-script&callback=showpageCount2&max-results=99999" ><\/script>')
                    }

           Call CreateButton(1501)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton16P.Value Then
            Call G_Report1601
           Call CreateButton(1601)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton17P.Value Then
            
            Call G_Report1701
           Call CreateButton(1701)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        
'        If .OptionButton18P.Value Then
'            Call G_Report1801
'           Call CreateButton(1801)
'           Call CreateBack
'        End If
        
        If .OptionButton10P1.Value Then
            Call G_Report1001
           Call CreateButton(1001)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton10P2.Value Then
            Call G_Report1002
           Call CreateButton(1002)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton10P3.Value Then
            Call G_Report1003
           Call CreateButton(1003)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton10P4.Value Then
            Call G_Report1004
           Call CreateButton(1004)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton11P.Value Then
            Call G_Report1101
           Call CreateButton(1101)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton12P1.Value Then
            Call G_Report1201
           Call CreateButton(1201)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton12P2.Value Then
            Call G_Report1202
           Call CreateButton(1202)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton12P3.Value Then
            Call G_Report1203
           Call CreateButton(1203)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton12P4.Value Then
            Call G_Report1204
           Call CreateButton(1204)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
        If .OptionButton12P5.Value Then
            Call G_Report1205
           Call CreateButton(1205)
           Call CreateBack
        End If
    End With
    
    Range("A1").Select
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub
Function G_Validate()
    G_Validate = False
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        
        If .cbo_Data.Enabled And .cbo_Data.Value = "" Then
            Exit Function
        End If
        
        If .cbo_Entity.Enabled And .cbo_Entity.Value = "" Then
            Exit Function
        End If
        
        If .cbo_Entity1.Enabled And .cbo_Entity1.Value = "" Then
            Exit Function
        End If
        
    End With
    G_Validate = True
End Function
Sub G_Report1() ' 01a. Volume Price Split (Brand)

    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Year As String
    Dim LStr_Scenario As String
    Dim LStr_YTD As String
    Dim LStr_Version As String
    
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    LStr_Worksheet = "01a. Volume Price Split (Brand)"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "01a. UploadWS"
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    End If
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("01a.B").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("4").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        
        'drop down list for month
        Range("I7").Select
        ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "Jul"
        Range("I7").Select
        Selection.AutoFill Destination:=Range("I7:I19"), Type:=xlFillDefault
        Range("I7:I18").Select
        'Range("I19").Select
        'ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "#Missing"
        Range("D7").Select
        With Selection.Validation
        .Delete
        .Add Type:=xlValidateList, AlertStyle:=xlValidAlertStop, Operator:= _
        xlBetween, Formula1:="=$I$7:$I$18"
        .IgnoreBlank = True
        .InCellDropdown = True
        .InputTitle = ""
        .ErrorTitle = ""
        .InputMessage = ""
        .ErrorMessage = ""
        .ShowInput = True
        .ShowError = True
        End With
    
        Range("D7").Select
        Selection.Copy
        Range("D8:D65535").Select
        ActiveSheet.Paste
        Range("C7").Select
        
    'hidden working rows and columns
        Columns("I:I").Select
        Selection.EntireColumn.Hidden = True

        Rows("1:1").Select
        Selection.EntireRow.Hidden = True
    'freeze area
        Range("C7").Select
        ActiveWindow.FreezePanes = True
        
    'format sheet
    Sheets("Main").Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    End With


    Set Sys_EssObj = Nothing
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub

Sub G_Report2() ' 01b. Volume Price Split (BrandPack)

    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet2 As String
    Dim LStr_Year As String
    Dim LStr_Scenario As String
    Dim LStr_YTD As String
    Dim LStr_Version As String
    
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    LStr_Worksheet = "01b. Volume Price Split (BP)"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "01b. UploadWS"
    LStr_Worksheet2 = "01b.B (2)"
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        'Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    End If
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet, True) Then
         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("01b.B").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("4").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Rows("4").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole
    
    End With
    
    'drop down list for month
    Range("L7").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "Jul"
    Range("L7").Select
    Selection.AutoFill Destination:=Range("L7:L18"), Type:=xlFillDefault
    Range("L7:L18").Select
    'Range("L19").Select
    'ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "#Missing"
    Range("D7").Select
    With Selection.Validation
        .Delete
        .Add Type:=xlValidateList, AlertStyle:=xlValidAlertStop, Operator:= _
        xlBetween, Formula1:="=$L$7:$L$18"
        .IgnoreBlank = True
        .InCellDropdown = True
        .InputTitle = ""
        .ErrorTitle = ""
        .InputMessage = ""
        .ErrorMessage = ""
        .ShowInput = True
        .ShowError = True
    End With
    Range("D7").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Range("D8:D65535").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    'Range("G12").Select
    
    'hidden working rows and columns
        Columns("L:L").Select
        Selection.EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        
        Rows("1:1").Select
        Selection.EntireRow.Hidden = True
        
    'freeze area
        Range("C7").Select
        ActiveWindow.FreezePanes = True
        
    'format sheet
    Sheets("Main").Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False

    
    Set Sys_EssObj = Nothing
'Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub

    Dim LStr_Scenario As String
    Dim LStr_YTD As String

    LStr_Worksheet1 = "03. UploadWS"
    
     If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)

Sub G_Report93() '5ac. SPTD (Target Incentive)
    
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Year As String
    Dim LStr_Scenario As String
    Dim LStr_YTD As String
    Dim LStr_Version As String
    
    
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    LStr_Worksheet = "05ac. Target Incentive"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "05ac. UploadWS"
    
     If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    End If
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet, True) Then
         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("05ac.B").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        LStr_Scenario = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O9").Value
        Rows("3").Replace what:="LE1", Replacement:=LStr_Scenario, LookAt:=xlPart
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("4").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        
    End With

Sub G_Report114() '06ab. A&D (SSA)
    
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Year As String
    Dim LStr_Scenario As String
    Dim LStr_YTD As String
    Dim LStr_Version As String
    
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    LStr_Worksheet = "06ab. A&D (SSA)"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "06ab. UploadWS"
    
     If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    End If
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet, True) Then
         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("06ab.B").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        LStr_Scenario = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O9").Value
        Rows("3").Replace what:="LE1", Replacement:=LStr_Scenario, LookAt:=xlPart
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("4").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        
    End With
    
    'drop down list for currency
    Range("BB7").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "AUD"

         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("08.B").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        LStr_Scenario = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O9").Value
        Rows("3").Replace what:="LE1", Replacement:=LStr_Scenario, LookAt:=xlPart
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("4").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole

Sub G_Report15() '12a. Structure Costs
    
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Year As String
    Dim LStr_Scenario As String
    Dim LStr_YTD As String
    Dim LStr_Version As String
    Dim LStr_Entity As String
    
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    LStr_Worksheet = "12a. Structure Costs"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "12a. UploadWS"
    
     If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    End If
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet, True) Then
         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("12a.B").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        LStr_Scenario = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O9").Value
        Rows("3").Replace what:="LE1", Replacement:=LStr_Scenario, LookAt:=xlPart
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("4").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        'LStr_Entity = .cbo_Entity.Value
        'Range("B4").Select
        'ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = LStr_Entity
        'Range("C6").Select
    End With
    
    'drop down list for Entity
    Range("S7").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "PRADF"
    Range("S8").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "PRCDF"
    Range("S9").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "PRJDF"
'    Range("S10").Select
'    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "NA"
    
    Range("B7").Select
    With Selection.Validation
        .Delete
        .Add Type:=xlValidateList, AlertStyle:=xlValidAlertStop, Operator:= _
        xlBetween, Formula1:="=$S$7:$S$9"
        .IgnoreBlank = True
        .InCellDropdown = True
        .InputTitle = ""
        .ErrorTitle = ""
        .InputMessage = ""
        .ErrorMessage = ""
        .ShowInput = True
        .ShowError = True
    End With
    
    Range("B7").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Range("B8:B65535").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Range("D7").Select
    
    
    'hidden working rows and columns
        
        Rows("1:1").Select
        Selection.EntireRow.Hidden = True
   
    'freeze area
        Range("D7").Select
        ActiveWindow.FreezePanes = True
        
    'format sheet
    Sheets("Main").Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False

   
    Set Sys_EssObj = Nothing
'Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub

Sub G_Report1001() '05ab. SPTD (9L)
    
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Year As String
    Dim LStr_Scenario As String
    Dim LStr_YTD As String
    Dim LStr_Version As String
    
    
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    LStr_Worksheet = "05ab. SPTD (9L)"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "05ab. UploadWSF"
    
     If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    End If
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet, True) Then
         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("05ab.P").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("3").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
    End With
    
    'drop down list for currency
    Range("J7").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "AUD"

    Dim LStr_YTD As String

    Application.ScreenUpdating = False

    LStr_Worksheet1 = "06aa. UploadWSF"
    
     If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    End If
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet, True) Then
         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("06aa.P").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("3").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole

        xlBetween, Formula1:="=$J$7:$J$50"
        .IgnoreBlank = True
        .InCellDropdown = True
        .InputTitle = ""
        .ErrorTitle = ""
        .InputMessage = ""
        .ErrorMessage = ""
        .ShowInput = True
        .ShowError = True
    End With

    Selection.Copy
    Range("C7:C65535").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Range("C7").Select

        Rows("1:1").Select
        Selection.EntireRow.Hidden = True

        Columns("J:J").Select
        Selection.EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        
    'freeze area
        Range("C7").Select
        ActiveWindow.FreezePanes = True
        
    'format sheet
    Sheets("Main").Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False

   
    Set Sys_EssObj = Nothing
'Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub

Sub G_Report1301() '07.Handling Costs
    
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Year As String
    Dim LStr_Scenario As String
    Dim LStr_YTD As String
    Dim LStr_Version As String
    
    
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    LStr_Worksheet = "07. Handling Costs"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "07. UploadWSF"
    
     If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet1, True) Then
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet1
    End If
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    
    If Find_WS_Exists(LStr_Worksheet, True) Then
         Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Delete
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
        Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Else
        Worksheets.Add After:=Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        ActiveSheet.Name = LStr_Worksheet
    End If
    
    ' build template
    Worksheets("07.P").Cells.Copy
    Range("A" & "1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    
    With Worksheets(GStr_MainSht)
        
        LStr_Year = Worksheets(GStr_MainSht).Range("O8").Value
        Rows("2").Replace what:="FY14", Replacement:=LStr_Year, LookAt:=xlWhole
        
        LStr_YTD = getCboValue(.cbo_Data)
        Rows("3").Replace what:="Int", Replacement:=LStr_YTD, LookAt:=xlWhole
       
    End With
    
    'hidden working rows and columns
        
        Rows("1:1").Select
        Selection.EntireRow.Hidden = True

    'freeze area
        Range("C7").Select
        ActiveWindow.FreezePanes = True
        
    'format sheet
    Sheets("Main").Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False

   
    Set Sys_EssObj = Nothing
'Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub

Sub Back()
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False
    Sheets("Main").Visible = True
    ActiveSheet.Delete
    Worksheets("Main").Select
End Sub
Sub CreateBack()
    ActiveSheet.Buttons.Add(30, 30, 60, 20).Select
    Selection.Name = "BackMain"
    Selection.OnAction = "Back"
    ActiveSheet.Shapes("BackMain").Select
    Selection.Characters.Text = "Main Page"

End Sub

Sub Upload()
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim x As Long
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    

    LStr_Worksheet = "01a. UploadWS"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "01a. Volume Price Split (Brand)"
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False

    'create upload WS
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Cells.Select
    Selection.ClearContents
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C1:F6").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("C1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A7:E65535").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("A7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'replace drop down value
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Jul", Replacement:="1", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Aug", Replacement:="2", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Sep", Replacement:="3", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Oct", Replacement:="4", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Nov", Replacement:="5", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Dec", Replacement:="6", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Jan", Replacement:="7", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Feb", Replacement:="8", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Mar", Replacement:="9", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Apr", Replacement:="10", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="May", Replacement:="11", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Jun", Replacement:="12", LookAt:=xlPart

  ' Essbase part
    Call EssSys(LStr_Worksheet)

    ' Launch Business Rules
    x = EssVCalculate(Empty, "Form_Vol_B", False)
    
    'format sheet
    

    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C7").Select
   
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    
End Sub

Sub Upload2()
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet2 As String
    Dim x As Long
    Dim LLng_BottomRow As Long
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    LStr_Worksheet = "01b. UploadWS"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "01b. Volume Price Split (BP)"
    LStr_Worksheet2 = "01b.B (2)"
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False

    'create upload WS
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Cells.Select
    Selection.ClearContents
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    Range("C1:H6").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("C1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A7:B65535").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("A7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
        
    'Essbase Retrieve Org and Adjs
    Call EssSysRetrieve(LStr_Worksheet)
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("B7:D65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("B7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'replace drop down value
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Jul", Replacement:="1", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Aug", Replacement:="2", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Sep", Replacement:="3", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Oct", Replacement:="4", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Nov", Replacement:="5", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Dec", Replacement:="6", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Jan", Replacement:="7", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Feb", Replacement:="8", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Mar", Replacement:="9", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Apr", Replacement:="10", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="May", Replacement:="11", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("D").Replace what:="Jun", Replacement:="12", LookAt:=xlPart

    'Find last row
    LLng_BottomRow = Find_Last_Row("B", False)
    
    'Replace # Missing
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Cells.Select
    Selection.Replace what:="#Missing", Replacement:="", LookAt:=xlPart, _
    SearchOrder:=xlByRows, MatchCase:=False, SearchFormat:=False, _
    ReplaceFormat:=False
    
    'Create Formula
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("F7").Select
    ActiveCell.Value = "=C7-E7"
    Range("F7").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Range("F7:F" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste

    ' Essbase part

Sub Upload3()
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet2 As String
    Dim x As Long
    Dim LLng_BottomRow As Long

    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    LStr_Worksheet = "01c. UploadWS"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "01c. Volume Alloc (YT - Brand)"
    LStr_Worksheet2 = "1cB (2)"


    Application.DisplayAlerts = False

    'create upload WS
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Cells.Select
    Selection.ClearContents
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    Range("C1:F6").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("C1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A7:B65535").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("A7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C2:C5").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("D2:E2").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste

    
    'Essbase Retrieve Org and Adjs
    Call EssSysRetrieve(LStr_Worksheet)
    
     'Copy After Adj
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C7:C65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("C7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'Find last row
    LLng_BottomRow = Find_Last_Row("B", False)
    
    'Replace # Missing
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Cells.Select
    Selection.Replace what:="#Missing", Replacement:="", LookAt:=xlPart, _
    SearchOrder:=xlByRows, MatchCase:=False, SearchFormat:=False, _
    ReplaceFormat:=False
    
    'Create Formula
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("E7").Select
    ActiveCell.Value = "=C7-D7"
    Range("E7").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
        
    Range("E7:E" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    

    ' Essbase part
    Call EssSys(LStr_Worksheet)
    
    ' Launch Business Rules
    x = EssVCalculate(Empty, "Form_Vol_B", False)
    
    'format sheet
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C7").Select

    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

Sub Upload6() '02. Price
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim x As Long

    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    LStr_Worksheet = "02. UploadWS"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "02. Price"


    Application.DisplayAlerts = False

    'create upload WS
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Cells.Select
    Selection.ClearContents
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C1:G5").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("C1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A6:F65535").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("A6").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'replace drop down value
    Columns("C").Replace what:="AUD", Replacement:="1", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="CNY", Replacement:="2", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="EUR", Replacement:="3", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="GBP", Replacement:="4", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="HKD", Replacement:="5", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="JPY", Replacement:="6", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="KRW", Replacement:="7", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="MYR", Replacement:="8", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="NZD", Replacement:="9", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="SEK", Replacement:="10", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="SGD", Replacement:="11", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="THB", Replacement:="12", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="TWD", Replacement:="13", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="USD", Replacement:="14", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="ARS", Replacement:="15", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="MXN", Replacement:="16", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="VND", Replacement:="17", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="IDR", Replacement:="18", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="IND", Replacement:="19", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="LKR", Replacement:="20", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="PHP", Replacement:="21", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="FJD", Replacement:="22", LookAt:=xlPart
   
    ' Essbase part
    Call EssSys(LStr_Worksheet)

Sub Upload7() ' 03. Transfer Price
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim x As Long
    Dim InputEntity As String


    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    LStr_Worksheet = "03. UploadWS"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "03. Transfer Price"


    Application.DisplayAlerts = False

    'create upload WS
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Cells.Select
    Selection.ClearContents
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("B1:AV7").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("B1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A8:AV65535").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("A8").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'PRADF_Input
   InputEntity = Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Range("A6").Value
   Range("F1").Select
   ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = InputEntity & "_Input"
   Range("B8").Select
   
    
    'replace drop down value
    
    Range("B:B,F:F,J:J,N:N,R:R,V:V,Z:Z,AD:AD,AH:AH,AL:AL,AP:AP,AT:AT").Select

    
    Selection.Replace what:="AUD", Replacement:="1", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="CNY", Replacement:="2", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="EUR", Replacement:="3", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="GBP", Replacement:="4", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="HKD", Replacement:="5", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="JPY", Replacement:="6", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="KRW", Replacement:="7", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="MYR", Replacement:="8", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="NZD", Replacement:="9", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="SEK", Replacement:="10", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="SGD", Replacement:="11", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="THB", Replacement:="12", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="TWD", Replacement:="13", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="USD", Replacement:="14", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="ARS", Replacement:="15", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="MXN", Replacement:="16", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="VND", Replacement:="17", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="IDR", Replacement:="18", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="IND", Replacement:="19", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="LKR", Replacement:="20", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="PHP", Replacement:="21", LookAt:=xlPart
    Selection.Replace what:="FJD", Replacement:="22", LookAt:=xlPart
    
    
    ' Essbase part
    Call EssSys(LStr_Worksheet)

    ' Launch Business Rules

Sub Upload501() '01b. Volume Alloc(Cust Brand)
    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet2 As String
    Dim x As Long
    Dim LLng_BottomRow As Long

    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    LStr_Worksheet = "01b. UploadWSF"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "01b. Volume Alloc(Cust Brand)"
    LStr_Worksheet2 = "01b.P (2)"


    Application.DisplayAlerts = False

    'create upload WS
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Cells.Select
    Selection.ClearContents
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    Range("C1:J6").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("C1").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A7:B65535").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("A7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C2:C4").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("D2:F2:G2:I2:J2").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
      
    
    'Essbase Retrieve Org and Adjs
    Call EssSysRetrieve(LStr_Worksheet)
    
    'Copy After Adj
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C7:C65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("E7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("D7:D65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("H7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("E7:E65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("K7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'Find last row
    LLng_BottomRow = Find_Last_Row("B", False)
    
    'Replace # Missing
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Cells.Select
    Selection.Replace what:="#Missing", Replacement:="", LookAt:=xlPart, _
    SearchOrder:=xlByRows, MatchCase:=False, SearchFormat:=False, _
    ReplaceFormat:=False
    
    
    'Create Formula
    
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("D7").Select
    ActiveCell.Value = "=SUM(E7,-C7)"
    Range("D7").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Range("D7:D" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("G7").Select
    ActiveCell.Value = "=SUM(H7,-F7)"
    Range("G7").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Range("G7:G" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("J7").Select
    ActiveCell.Value = "=SUM(K7,-I7)"
    Range("J7").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Range("J7:J" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    
    ' Essbase part
    Call EssSys(LStr_Worksheet)

    ' Launch Business Rules
    x = EssVCalculate(Empty, "Form_Vol_Ini_5YP", False)

    'format sheet
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C7").Select

    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A7:B65535").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("A7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C2:C4").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("D2:F2:G2:I2:J2").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'Essbase Retrieve Org and Adjs
    Call EssSysRetrieve(LStr_Worksheet)
    
    'Copy After Adj
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C7:C65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("E7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("D7:D65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("H7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("E7:E65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("K7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'Find last row
    LLng_BottomRow = Find_Last_Row("B", False)
    
    'Replace # Missing
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Cells.Select
    Selection.Replace what:="#Missing", Replacement:="", LookAt:=xlPart, _
    SearchOrder:=xlByRows, MatchCase:=False, SearchFormat:=False, _
    ReplaceFormat:=False
    
    
    'Create Formula
    
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("D7").Select
    ActiveCell.Value = "=SUM(E7,-C7)"
    Range("D7").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Range("D7:D" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("G7").Select
    ActiveCell.Value = "=SUM(H7,-F7)"
    Range("G7").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Range("G7:G" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("J7").Select
    ActiveCell.Value = "=SUM(K7,-I7)"
    Range("J7").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Range("J7:J" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    

    ' Essbase part
    Call EssSys(LStr_Worksheet)

    ' Launch Business Rules
    x = EssVCalculate(Empty, "Form_Vol_Ini_5YP", False)

    'format sheet
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet2).Select
    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C7").Select

    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True

    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim x As Long

    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    LStr_Worksheet = "02. UploadWSF"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "02. Price"

    
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False

    'create upload WS
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Cells.Select

    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("C1").Select

    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A7:J65535").Select
    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet).Select
    Range("A7").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste

    Columns("C").Replace what:="CNY", Replacement:="2", LookAt:=xlPart

    Columns("C").Replace what:="GBP", Replacement:="4", LookAt:=xlPart

    Columns("C").Replace what:="KRW", Replacement:="7", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="MYR", Replacement:="8", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="NZD", Replacement:="9", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="SEK", Replacement:="10", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="SGD", Replacement:="11", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="THB", Replacement:="12", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="TWD", Replacement:="13", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="USD", Replacement:="14", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="ARS", Replacement:="15", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="MXN", Replacement:="16", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="VND", Replacement:="17", LookAt:=xlPart
     Columns("C").Replace what:="IDR", Replacement:="18", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="IND", Replacement:="19", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="LKR", Replacement:="20", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="PHP", Replacement:="21", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="FJD", Replacement:="22", LookAt:=xlPart

    Columns("C").Replace what:="PHP", Replacement:="21", LookAt:=xlPart
    Columns("C").Replace what:="FJD", Replacement:="22", LookAt:=xlPart

    ' Essbase part
    Call EssSys(LStr_Worksheet)
    
    ' Launch Business Rules
    x = EssVCalculate(Empty, "Form_AD_Pct_5YP", False)
        
    'format sheet

    ActiveWindow.SelectedSheets.Visible = False
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("C7").Select

    Application.CutCopyMode = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True

Sub EssSys(LStr_Worksheet As String)

'Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
Dim x As Long

'LStr_Worksheet = "01. UploadWS"

G_NewEssObj
    With Sys_EssObj
        .G_SetSheetOption LStr_Worksheet
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 13, False) 'use alias
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 24, False) 'both member and alias
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 6, False) 'suppress missing
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 7, False)  'suppress zero
        x = EssVSetGlobalOption(6, False) 'Set Display-unknown settings to "off"

        
        x = .Connect(LStr_Worksheet, Sys_AcctApp, Sys_AcctDb)
        If x = GInt_SuccessCode Then
        
            
            x = .SendData(LStr_Worksheet)
            x = .Retrieve(LStr_Worksheet)
            'MsgBox "1"
        End If
       
    End With
    G_NewEssObj
    With Sys_EssObj
        .G_SetSheetOption LStr_Worksheet
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 13, False) 'use alias
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 24, False) 'both member and alias
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 6, False) 'suppress missing
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 7, False)  'suppress zero
        x = EssVSetGlobalOption(5, 2) 'Set Message level to "Warnings Messages Only"

        
        x = .Connect(LStr_Worksheet, Sys_AcctApp, Sys_AcctDb)
        If x = GInt_SuccessCode Then
           
            x = .SendData(LStr_Worksheet)
            x = EssVSetGlobalOption(6, True) 'Set Display-unknown settings to "on"
            x = .Retrieve(LStr_Worksheet)
            'MsgBox "2"
        End If
       
    End With

'    MsgBox "Uploaded all vaild records"

End Sub
