Sub EssSysRetrieve(LStr_Worksheet As String)

    Dim x As Long


    G_NewEssObj
    With Sys_EssObj
        .G_SetSheetOption LStr_Worksheet
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 13, False) 'use alias
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 24, False) 'both member and alias
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 6, False) 'suppress missing
        x = .SetSheetOption(LStr_Worksheet, 7, False)  'suppress zero
        x = EssVSetGlobalOption(6, False) 'Set Display-unknown settings to "off"

        
        x = .Connect(LStr_Worksheet, Sys_AcctApp, Sys_AcctDb)
        If x = GInt_SuccessCode Then
        
            
            'x = .SendData(LStr_Worksheet)
            x = .Retrieve(LStr_Worksheet)
            'MsgBox "1"
        End If
       
    End With
    

End Sub



Sub VolumeAdj()

    Dim LStr_Worksheet As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet1 As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet2 As String
    Dim LStr_Worksheet3 As String
    Dim x As Long
    Dim LLng_BottomRow As Long
    'Dim LStr_Col As String

    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    LStr_Worksheet = "01e. UploadWS"
    LStr_Worksheet1 = "01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)"
    LStr_Worksheet2 = "01e.B (3)"
    LStr_Worksheet3 = "01e.B (4)"
    
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet3).Visible = True
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet3).Select
    
    Worksheets(LStr_Worksheet1).Select
    Range("A8:B65535").Select
    Selection.Copy
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet3).Select
    Range("A8").Select
    ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    Call EssSysRetrieve(LStr_Worksheet3)
    
    'Replace # Missing
    Sheets(LStr_Worksheet3).Cells.Select
    Selection.Replace what:="#Missing", Replacement:="", LookAt:=xlPart, _
    SearchOrder:=xlByRows, MatchCase:=False, SearchFormat:=False, _
    ReplaceFormat:=False
        
    'Find last row
    LLng_BottomRow = Find_Last_Row("B", False)
    
    'create formula
    'Jul
        Range("E8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!D8"
        Range("E8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("E8:E" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
        ActiveSheet.Paste
    'Aug
        Range("J8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!G8"
        Range("J8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("J8:J" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
        ActiveSheet.Paste
    
    'Sep
        Range("O8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!J8"
        Range("O8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("O8:O" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
        ActiveSheet.Paste
        
    'Oct
        Range("T8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!M8"
        Range("T8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("T8:T" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
        ActiveSheet.Paste
        
    'Nov
        Range("Y8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!P8"
        Range("Y8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("Y8:Y" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
        
    'Dec
        Range("AD8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!S8"
        Range("AD8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("AD8:AD" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
        
    'Jan
        Range("AI8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!V8"
        Range("AI8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("AI8:AI" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
        
    'Feb
        Range("AN8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!Y8"
        Range("AN8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("AN8:AN" & LLng_BottomRow).Select
        
    'Mar
        Range("AS8").Select
        ActiveCell.Value = "='01e. Volume Adj (Month - BP)'!AB8"
        Range("AS8").Select
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        Selection.Copy
        Range("AS8:AS" & LLng_BottomRow).Select

list<ASI_MFM_Payment__c> ph_list = [select ID,ASI_MFM_Payment_Amount__c,
                                    (select ASI_MFM_Payment_Amount__c,ASI_MFM_PO_Line_Item__r.ASI_MFM_PO__r.ASI_MFM_Plan__c from Payment_Line_Items__r) 
                                    from ASI_MFM_Payment__c where RecordType.DeveloperName LIKE 'ASI_MFM_KR%'];



for (ASI_MFM_Payment__c ph:ph_list) {
    
    decimal amount=0;
    for (ASI_MFM_Payment_Line_Item__c pi:ph.Payment_Line_Items__r) {
        if (pi.ASI_MFM_Payment_Amount__c != null) {
            amount += pi.ASI_MFM_Payment_Amount__c;
        }
    }
    
    if(amount!=ph.ASI_MFM_Payment_Amount__c){
        ph.ASI_MFM_Payment_Amount__c = amount;
    }
}

update ph_list;

//Start checking 
for (var pol in POLineMap) { 
if(typeof PlanLineMap[pol] =='undefined'){ 
Message =POLineMap[pol].name+': Cannot find in Plan Line.'; 
issub=false; 
isprocess=false; 
}else{ 
if(Number(POLineMap[pol].amount)>(Number(PlanLineMap[pol].amount)*(1+Tolerance/100))){ 
console.log('AC Code: '+POLineMap[pol].name+' Over Budget: Plan Amount : '+ Number(PlanLineMap[pol].amount)*(1+Tolerance/100)+ 'PO Amount: '+Number(POLineMap[pol].amount) ); 
Message +='AC Code: '+POLineMap[pol].name+' Over Budget.\n'; 
issub=false; 
isprocess=false; 
} 
} 

} 

//show error message 
if(!isprocess){ 
alert(Message); 
} 
} 

} 

} // End OF 'F' Plan checking 

if(po.ASI_MFM_Plan__r.ASI_MFM_Prefix__r.ASI_MFM_Over_Spending_Checking__c!='false'){ 
if(po.ASI_MFM_Plan__r.ASI_MFM_Plan_Amount__c>0){ 
var balance=(po.ASI_MFM_Plan__r.ASI_MFM_Plan_Balance__c-po.ASI_MFM_Base_Currency_Amount__c)/po.ASI_MFM_Plan__r.ASI_MFM_Plan_Amount__c; 
var Tolerance=0; 
if(po.ASI_MFM_Plan__r.ASI_MFM_Prefix__r.ASI_MFM_Tolerance__c==null){ 
Tolerance=0; 
}else{ 
Tolerance=po.ASI_MFM_Plan__r.ASI_MFM_Prefix__r.ASI_MFM_Tolerance__c 
} 
if(balance<0){	
if(Math.abs(balance)>(Tolerance/100)){ 
alert('PO Amount greater than Tolerance. Cannot Submit for Approval.'); 
issub=false; 
} 
} 
}else{ 
alert('Amount Cannot Be Smallar Than 0'); 
issub=false; 
} 
}//End checking 


if(issub){ 
if ((Modal.confirm && Modal.confirm('Once you submit this record for approval, you might not be able to edit it or recall it from the approval process depending on your settings. Continue?')) || (!Modal.confirm && window.confirm('Once you submit this record for approval, you might not be able to edit it or recall it from the approval process depending on your settings. Continue?'))) 
navigateToUrl('/apex/ASI_SubmitApprovalPage?id={!ASI_MFM_PO__c.Id}'); 
} 

}






















public with sharing class ASI_CRM_KR_ListedPriceUploadCtrl {
    
    public String report_PriorityItem {get;set;} //For Report generation
    public String report_TempDataReport {get;set;} //For Report generation
    public ASI_MFM_Mass_Upload_Log__c MFMlog {set;get;}
    public Id BatchId {set;get;}
    
    public String Msg1 {get;set;}
    
    public string[] GenStatusMsgs{
       
        get{
            string s = Msg1 ==null? '': Msg1;
            return s.split('\n');
        }
        
    }
    
    public boolean DeletePermission {get;set;} {DeletePermission = false;}
    public boolean DeleteMsg {get;set;} {DeleteMsg = false;}
    
        
    public ASI_CRM_KR_ListedPriceUploadCtrl(){
        report_PriorityItem = retrievePriorityItemReport('KR_CRM_Item_Group_PriorityItem');
        report_TempDataReport = retrievePriorityItemReport('ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPriceReport');
    }
    
    //start
    public class interimData { 
                ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c create_Header {set;get;}    
                ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c create_Line {set;get;}  
            }
    public List<ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c> TempDataList =new List<ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c> (); //storing temp listing data
            public Set<string> SearchOldListingIDSet =new Set<string> ();  //for storing old Listing Header Key
            public Set<string> OldListingIDSet =new Set<string> ();
            public List<ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c> UpsertLineList =new List<ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c> (); //for insert/update
            
            public List<ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c> InsertListingHeaderList =new List<ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c> ();
            public Map<string,interimData> InsertListingLineMap =new Map<string,interimData> ();
            public Map<ID,ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c> AfterInsetHeaderMap =new Map<ID,ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c> (); 
            public List<ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c> ListingLineList =new List<ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c> ();   // Insert SIT Line
    
    //end        
            
    private String retrievePriorityItemReport(String repRecType){
        String reportType = '#';
        List<Report> report = [Select Id, Name, DeveloperName From Report Where DeveloperName =: repRecType];
        
        if(report.size() > 0){
            
            if(repRecType == 'KR_CRM_Item_Group_PriorityItem'){
                reportType = '/' + report[0].Id + '?export=1&enc=UTF-8&xf=xls';
            }
            else{
                 reportType = '/' + report[0].Id;
            }
        }
        
        return reportType;
    }
    
    public void generateHeader(){
        DeleteMsg = false;
        DeletePermission = false; 
        MFMlog= new ASI_MFM_Mass_Upload_Log__c();
        
        list<ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c> templine1  = [select id from ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c limit 1];
        if(templine1.size() > 0 && templine1 != null){
            
            insert MFMlog;
            //BatchId= Database.executeBatch(new ASI_CRM_KR_ListingUploadBatch(MFMlog),500);  
            
            
            //start
            System.Savepoint sp = database.setSavepoint();
            Map<string,string> ListingHeader_Key_ID_List = new Map<string,string> (); 
            Set<string> HeaderIdSet =new Set<string> ();
            
            for(ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c TempDataListRecord :[select id, ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c,ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c, ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c, ASI_CRM_KR_Item_Group_Code__c, ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Price__c,ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c
                                                                       from ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c ]){
                string TempDataListRecordASI_CRM_KR_Venue;                                                         
                if(string.valueof(TempDataListRecord.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c).length() > 15){
                     TempDataListRecordASI_CRM_KR_Venue = (string.valueof(TempDataListRecord.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c)).left(15);
                }                                                          
                String HeaderID = TempDataListRecord.ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c + '_'+  TempDataListRecord.ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c + '_'+ TempDataListRecordASI_CRM_KR_Venue ;
                
                SearchOldListingIDSet.add(HeaderID);  
                TempDataList.add(TempDataListRecord);  
                
            }
           //system.assertEquals(TempDataList,null);
           
            
          //Prepare Existing Listed Menu Price Entries List
         for(ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c oldListingHeader : [select id, ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c
                                                                from ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c 
                                                                where ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c in: SearchOldListingIDSet and recordtype.developername = 'ASI_CRM_KR']){
            OldListingIDSet.add(oldListingHeader.ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c);  //Put all external ID in OldListingIDSet
            ListingHeader_Key_ID_List.put(oldListingHeader.ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c,oldListingHeader.id);
        }
        
        
        
        for(ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c templine : TempDataList){
            string templineASI_CRM_KR_Venue;                                                         
                if(string.valueof(templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c).length() > 15){
                     templineASI_CRM_KR_Venue = (string.valueof(templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c)).left(15);
                }      
            
            String HeaderID = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c + '_'+ templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c  + '_' +   templineASI_CRM_KR_Venue;   
            
            if(OldListingIDSet.contains(HeaderID)){ //Header is already created, no need to create Header for that temp ine
                UpsertLineList.add(templine);
                //system.assertEquals(UpsertLineList,null);
            }
            else{
                
                //Need to create Listing Header since there is no existing Listing Header
                if(!HeaderIdSet.contains(HeaderID)){
                     
                    HeaderIdSet.add(HeaderID);
                    interimData temp =new interimData();
                    
                    ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c ListingHeader = new ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c(ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c,
                                                                                                       ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c,
                                                                                                       ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c);
                    temp.create_Header=ListingHeader;
                    InsertListingHeaderList.add(ListingHeader); //Put in InsertListingHeaderList for later inserting to database
                    
                    //Put data to Listing Line preparing for Listing Line Creation
                    interimData tempNew =new interimData();
                    tempNew.create_Line= new ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c(ASI_KOR_Item_Group_Code__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Item_Group_Code__c,
                                                                                 ASI_KOR_Listed_Price__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Price__c,
                                                                                 ASI_CRM_KR_HeaderID_Upload__c = HeaderID); //ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__c
                
                	InsertListingLineMap.put(templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c, tempNew);
                	SearchOldListingIDSet.add(HeaderID);
                }
                else{
                    // Put data to Listing Line preparing for Listing Line Creation
                    interimData tempNew =new interimData();
                    tempNew.create_Line= new ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c(ASI_KOR_Item_Group_Code__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Item_Group_Code__c,
                                                                                 ASI_KOR_Listed_Price__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Price__c,
                                                                                 ASI_CRM_KR_HeaderID_Upload__c = HeaderID); //ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__c
                    InsertListingLineMap.put(templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c, tempNew); 
                }
            }
        }
        //system.assertEquals(InsertListingLineMap,null);
        if(InsertListingHeaderList.size()>0){ 
            
            try{
                
                insert InsertListingHeaderList;   //Insert Header
                } catch (DmlException dmle) {
                MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Error_Message__c+= dmle.getMessage() ;
                database.rollback(sp);
                } catch (Exception e) {
                MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Error_Message__c+=e.getMessage() ;
                database.rollback(sp);
                
                } 
            
        }
        
        //------------------------------------------------------------Insert Listing Line-----------------------------------------------------//
        //Get Header ID after inserted for mapping Listing Line to Header
        
        //AfterInsetHeaderMap =new Map<ID,ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c> (); 
        for (ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c eachHeader : [select id, ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c,  ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c, ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c, ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c
                                                           from ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Price__c 
                                                           where ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c in: SearchOldListingIDSet and recordtype.developername = 'ASI_CRM_KR']){
            AfterInsetHeaderMap.put(eachHeader.id, eachHeader); 

        }
        
        for(String UPLOAD_ID : InsertListingLineMap.keyset()){ //InsertListingLineMap stores Listing Line that needs to create Listing line. Listing Header is just created
             
            ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c temp1 = InsertListingLineMap.get(UPLOAD_ID).create_line;
            
             for (String eachHeader : AfterInsetHeaderMap.keyset()){
                 
                 string MappingKey = string.valueOf(AfterInsetHeaderMap.get(eachHeader).ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c); 
                  SYSTEM.assertEquals(temp1.ASI_CRM_KR_HeaderID_Upload__c,NULL); //FY1617_Q4_001L000000p2VNcIAM = FY1617_Q4_001L000000p2VNc
                 if(temp1.ASI_CRM_KR_HeaderID_Upload__c == MappingKey){
                     
                     temp1.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__c = eachHeader;  
                     if(temp1.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__c != null){	       
                        ListingLineList.add(temp1);  
                    }
                 }
             }
        }
        
        if(ListingLineList.size() > 0 ){
            
            try{
                insert ListingLineList;
                MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Configuration__c = '';
                //log.ASI_MFM_Configuration__c +=  Temp_Map.size() + ' record(s) inserted.';
                MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Configuration__c =  ' record(s) upserted.';
            
            }catch (DmlException dmle) {
                //system.assertEquals(null,  dmle.getMessage());
                MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Error_Message__c+=dmle.getMessage() ;  
                database.rollback(sp);
            }catch (Exception e){
                //system.assertEquals(null, e);
                MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Error_Message__c+=e.getMessage() ;  
                database.rollback(sp);
            }
            
        }
        
        //--------------------------------- Update Line/Insert Line when the Header is already created before running this class -------------//
        if(SearchOldListingIDSet.size() > 0 ){
            List<ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c> InsertLineList  = new  List<ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c>();
            Map<String,ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c> CurrentLineMap  = new  Map<String,ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c>();
            List<ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c> UpdateLineMap  = new  List<ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c>();
            
            for(ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c templine : [select id,ASI_KOR_Item_Group_Code__c,
                                                                ASI_KOR_Listed_Price__c,
                                                                ASI_CRM_KR_HeaderID_Upload__c,
                                                                ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__r.ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c,
                                                                ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__r.ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c,
                                                                ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__r.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c
                                                                from ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c 
                                                                where ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__r.ASI_CRM_KR_Unique_ID__c in: SearchOldListingIDSet])
            { 
                string Line_uniqueKey = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__r.ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c + templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__r.ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c + templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__r.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c + templine.ASI_KOR_Item_Group_Code__c;                
                CurrentLineMap.put(Line_uniqueKey,templine);
            }
            
            if(CurrentLineMap.size() > 0){
                //Update Line
                for(ASI_CRM_KR_TempListedMenuPrice__c templine :UpsertLineList){
                    string templine_uniqueKey = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c + templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c + templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c  + templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Item_Group_Code__c ;
                    String HeaderID = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Fiscal_Year__c + templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Quarter__c + templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c ;
                    
                    if(CurrentLineMap.containsKey(templine_uniqueKey)){
                        //Update Line
                        CurrentLineMap.get(templine_uniqueKey).ASI_KOR_Listed_Price__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Price__c;
                        UpdateLineMap.add(CurrentLineMap.get(templine_uniqueKey));
                    }
                    
                    else{
                    //Insert Line
                    
                    string templineASI_CRM_KR_Venue;                                                         
                    if(string.valueof(templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c).length() > 15){
                         templineASI_CRM_KR_Venue = (string.valueof(templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c)).left(15);
                    }   
                
                    
                    interimData tempNew =new interimData();
                    
                    //system.assertEquals(ListingHeader_Key_ID_List, null);  //FY1617_Q2_001L000000p2VNc
                    //system.assertEquals(HeaderID, null);                    //FY1617_Q4_001L000000p2VNcIAM
                    
                    tempNew.create_Line= new ASI_KOR_Venue_Listed_Menu_Product__c(ASI_KOR_Listed_Price__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Price__c,
                                                                                 ASI_CRM_KR_Listed_Menu_Product_Header__c = ListingHeader_Key_ID_List.get(HeaderID),
                                                                                 ASI_KOR_ListedMenuProduct_to_Venue_Link__c= templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Venue__c,
                                                                                 ASI_KOR_Item_Group_Code__c = templine.ASI_CRM_KR_Item_Group_Code__c);
                    
                    InsertLineList.add(tempNew.create_Line);
                    
                    } 
                    
                }
                
            }
            
            //system.assertEquals(InsertLineList, null);
            if(InsertLineList.size() > 0 ){
                try{
                    insert InsertLineList;  
                    MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Configuration__c = ' record(s) upserted.';  
                    //system.assertEquals(InsertLineList,null);
                } 
                catch (DmlException dmle) {
                    MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Error_Message__c+= dmle.getMessage();
                    system.assertEquals(dmle.getMessage(),null);
                    database.rollback(sp);
                }
                catch (Exception e){
                
                    MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Error_Message__c+=e.getMessage();
                    system.assertEquals(e.getMessage(),null);
                    database.rollback(sp);
                }
                //system.assertEquals(null, SITLineList);
            }  
            
            if(UpdateLineMap.size() > 0 ){
                try{
                    update UpdateLineMap;
                    //log.ASI_MFM_Configuration__c +=  SITLineList.size() + ' record(s) updated.123';
                    MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Configuration__c = ' record(s) upserted.';
                    update MFMlog;
                }
                catch (DmlException dmle) {
                    //system.assertEquals(null,  dmle.getMessage());
                    MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Error_Message__c+= dmle.getMessage();
                    database.rollback(sp);
                }
                catch (Exception e){
                    
                    //system.assertEquals(null, e);
                    MFMlog.ASI_MFM_Error_Message__c+=e.getMessage();
                    database.rollback(sp);
                }
                //system.assertEquals(null, SITLineList);
            }
        }  
        //end
        }
        
        
    }
    
    public void deleteUploads(){
        
    }
}

        function addCalanderEvent(id,accid, start, end, title, colour, textColor, editable,type,DeveloperName)
        {
            
            var renderingtype='';
            var urllink='';
            if(type=='Holidays'){
                renderingtype='background';
            }
            
            if(type=='NewDate'){
                urllink='/'+accid;
            }else{
                urllink='/'+id;
            }
            
            var eventObject = {
                accid:accid,
                title: title,
                start: start,
                end: end,
                id: id,
                color: colour,
                textColor: textColor, 
                editable:  editable,
                rendering: renderingtype,
                type:type,
                DeveloperName:DeveloperName,
                tip:title, // For Mouseover event
                url:urllink
            };
            
            return eventObject;
        }
